рен/резрез/резреп, резрен:рейреж - Varsha Pai: Hey Guys,
I have released the Aptitude test. Make sure you take the test by 7 pm tomorrow. The test has 3 parts.
*Quants - 10 questions - 10 minutes 
*Verbal - 10 questions - 10 minutes 
*Logical - 10 questions - 10 minutes
*Aptitude Topics List*
*1.Quants:*
*Number System ( Divisibility Rule, Hcf and Lcm, Power cycle and Remainder cycle)
*Ratio and Proportions
*Percentages
*Profit and Loss
*Averages
*Mixtures and Alligations
*Time, Speed and Distance
*Permutation and Combination
*Probability
*Mensuration
*Logarithms
*Time and Work
*2.Logical*
* Number Series, Letter Series, Visual Reasoning
*Clocks and Calendars
*Cubes and Direction Sense
*Data Arrangements and Puzzles
*Blood Relations
*Data Interpretation and Data Sufficiency
*Coding and Decoding
*Algorithms and Flowchart
*Logical Deduction, Syllogisms, Venn diagrams
*3.Verbal:*
*Reading Comprehension
*Sentence Completion and Para jumbles
*Sentence Correction
*Articles and Prepositions
*Critical Reasoning
*Voice and Speech
*Vocabulary ( Synonym, Antonym, Idioms)
Please feel free to contact me if you need any further information.
